function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 304') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.304!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// File added: dev/index.html
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('dev/index.html', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('dev/index.html') && (sha1_file('dev/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/index.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/index.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/index.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/index.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('dev/index.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/index.html');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/index.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/index.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/index.html');
}

// Dir added: doc/developer_notes
@mkdir('doc/developer_notes');
if (!is_dir('doc/developer_notes')) {
	warn('Directory could not be created: doc/developer_notes');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change directory permissions of doc/developer_notes');
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != '3b219f678fe4f878f2676b336764a13bb9458981') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '3b219f678fe4f878f2676b336764a13bb9458981') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== 'ecbaf94c4f602b7ad7b8e75340c28cc9806840a9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '3b219f678fe4f878f2676b336764a13bb9458981') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}
